            <div class="sku-24-005-624" id="overview-content">
             <div class="banner">
             </div>
             <div class="main">
              <center>
               <img alt="29UM65-P" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/pro.jpg"/>
               <img alt="34UM65-P" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/pro2.jpg"/>
              </center>
              <h3 class="bt">
               Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking
              </h3>
              <strong>
               29UM65-P
              </strong>
              29" Class 21:9 UltraWide IPS Monitor (29.0" Diagonal)
              <br/>
              <strong>
               34UM65-P
              </strong>
              34" Class 21:9 UltraWide IPS Monitor (34.0" Diagonal)
              <p class="main-description">
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                UltraWide 21:9
               </li>
               <li>
                Mac Compatible
               </li>
               <li>
                sRGB 99%
               </li>
               <li>
                4-Screen Split
               </li>
              </ul>
              <div class="l-clear">
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="features l-staggered">
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="st">
               KEY FEATURES
              </div>
              <center>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a01.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a02.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a03.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a04.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a05.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a06.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a07.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a08.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a09.jpg"/>
               <img alt="icon" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/a10.jpg"/>
              </center>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/001.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                UltraWide 21:9
               </div>
               The UltraWide 21:9 aspect ratio makes movies and games more immersive than ever. Need to get some work done, too? All of that UltraWide real estate makes it easy to view multiple documents at the same time, so you don't need to flip back and forth between them.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-right" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/002.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                Mac Compatible
               </div>
               Graphic designers will surely appreciate the many features of LG's Mac-compatible UltraWide monitor. The 21:9 widescreen and 4-Screen Split will simplify working with multiple graphics windows. Disclaimer: Mac is a trademark of Apple, Inc. registered in the U.S. and other countries.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/003.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                sRGB 99%
               </div>
               sRGB is the standard color space of ideal color reproduction. So, with over 99% coverage of the sRGB spectrum, this LG monitor is a great solution for professional photographers, graphic designers or anyone looking for highly accurate color.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               *Disclaimer: Color mode conversion between Adobe RGB and sRGB is available on the "Color Mode" menu.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-right" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/004.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                Four-Screen Split
               </div>
               Multitasking doesn't have to mean shuffling back and forth between windows. With a single click, the 4-Screen Split feature divides the screen into as many as four customizable segments, two-by-two. Now you can see four different windows at the same time.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               Disclaimer: *Screen Split software runs on Windows Vista/7/8 and Mac OS.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/005.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                Dual Linkup
               </div>
               The Dual Linkup feature allows two compatible portable devices - such as a computer, camera, phone, or Blu-ray player - to be connected to the monitor, and both can be viewed on the same screen simultaneously.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-right" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/006.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                IPS
               </div>
               IPS (In-Plane Switching) technology enhances the performance of liquid crystal displays. Response times are shortened, color reproduction is improved, and users can now view the screen at virtually any angle.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/007.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                Full HD 1080p Resolution
               </div>
               This stunning picture is the reason you wanted HDTV in the first place. With almost double the pixel resolution, Full HD 1080p gives it superior picture quality over standard HDTV. You'll see details and colors like never before.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-right" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/008.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                ENERGY STAR-Qualified
               </div>
               Earning the ENERGY STAR means a product meets strict energy efficiency guidelines set by the US Environmental Protection Agency and the Department of Energy. For TVs, it means they save energy both in standby and active (when they're on) modes. ENERGY STAR qualified TVs use about 30% less energy than standard units.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              <div class="features-block">
               <img alt="Perfect for Gaming &amp; Multitasking" class="features-image l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/24/005/24-005-624/009.jpg"/>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="st">
                5M:1 Dynamic Contrast Ratio
               </div>
               A dynamic contrast ratio of 5,000,000:1 is your assurance of strong video performance, with deep blacks, bright whites and pleasing colors.
               <br style="clear:both;"/>
              </div>
              <div class="top-gradient">
              </div>
              You've probably never seen a monitor like LG's new UM65. The UltraWide screen boasts a 21:9 aspect ratio, so it's perfect for widescreen movies, or for displaying as many as four different windows simultaneously. Picture quality is appropriately amazing, with Full HD 1080p resolution, a dynamic contrast ratio of 5,000,000:1 and 99% coverage of the sRGB color space, plus IPS technology for a wide viewing angle. And this energy-efficient, Mac-compatible monitor offers versatile connectivity options.
             </div>

              <h3>
               <span class="itmRating">
                <img alt="4 out of 5 eggs" class="eggs r4" src="http://images10.newegg.com/WebResource/Themes/2005/Nest/none.gif"/>
                <span class="print" style="display:none;">
                 Rating: 4/5
                </span>
               </span>
               Nice upgrade from dual 24" monitors
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                You gain a lot of screen real estate and it flows better than using a dual monitor setup. Settings are easy to accomplish and there are lots of them! I like the ability to adjust (2) Reader settings for ease of eye strain, and viewing both the Mac mini and Windows PC on one screen is fantastic! The 4-split screen is useful to mulitask emails and social media too. The 2560 x 1080 looks good and was immediately recognized using a Windows 7 HDMI connection.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                The product shipped with only a Korean user manual! I had to go to the LG site to get the English version. Tilt only 5-20 degrees, no pivot or portrait mode available. Lost cut and paste capabilities with addition of dual screen software enabled in Windows 7. Must use DP connection on both monitor and Mac mini to gain expected resolution.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                The monitor I received had only a Korean user manual. I was able to get the English version off the LG site, in addition to the updated software for both Mac and Windows for split screen and dual link. Register product for 1 year warranty coverage.
               </p>
              </div>

               Fantastic
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                Going from 2 28" TN panels to this is a huge step up. The colors are defined, precise, and almost pop out. I can easily see the slightest difference in contrast now. I no longer have to be directly in line with my monitor to avoid color shifting. I reclaimed a ton of desk space with this monitor, I can see my speakers again! Love the clear stand, the monitor looks like it's floating if you don't notice the base. I have a window right beside my desk, I can open the shade completely and still see what's on the monitor perfectly now. The design of the monitor is beautiful, I almost feel like it should be hanging on the wall like a piece of art.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                It made me clean my desk, which was no easy task, thank you for telling me I'm a slob LG.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                Get it, you won't be dissapointed, unless you're like my ex, then nothing will ever fill the void where your soul should be, where was I, oh yea, the monitor is sublime!
               </p>

             <td>
              <div class="postdate">
              </div>
              <h3>
               <span class="itmRating">
                <img alt="5 out of 5 eggs" class="eggs r5" src="http://images10.newegg.com/WebResource/Themes/2005/Nest/none.gif"/>
                <span class="print" style="display:none;">
                 Rating: 5/5
                </span>
               </span>
               Exellent Monitor
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                I have owned for 4 months and I am still impressed with it. I purchased from a competitor because of store credit. Great multitask monitor. The resolution, while not as good as the 34UM95, is more than adequate for everyday tasks, gaming, and document editing. Two word documents or web pages will easily fit side by side for office productivity. Height is similar to a typical 27" monitor, and the width is about a 1/3 larger. Picture quality is outstanding. Connection inputs are also good. The lower resolution enables use with less powerful graphic cards.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                Photo/graphics editing may be the only activities where the superior resolution of the 34UM95 may be a must. Height does not adjust much and my be an issue. I experienced electrical back feed to the video card with computer shut down using the HDMI cable (LED's on video card were lit up with power off). Using duel link DVI cable or Display Port cable fixes this issue.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                Many reviews state that this monitor will not display at full resolution with the supplied HDMI cable. The 21:9 monitor is relatively new to the market. Older video cards may have trouble with this, particularly those built with HDMI 1.3 standards. I purchased a AMD R9 290 to drive this monitor and it set up and displayed flawlessly with HDMI.
                <br/>
                Also, some reviewers state being able to notice the individual pixels because of the resolution. They MUST be fogging the screen with their breath! With a typical setup on a desk, your not going to notice. My monitor does not suffer the backlight bleeding that some reviews speak either. Games and movies look awesome! I get average frame rates in newer games of between 45-60 or better with all filters and eye candy turned on and maxed out. Newer titles should adjust automatically. Older ones may not support 2560 x 1080 or play with a "stretched" 1920 x 1080 resolution. Windowed mode is always an option.
                <br/>
                This monitor is a bit pricey compared to a typical 27" dual monitor setup, but the overall experience is far better.
               </p>
              </div>
              <p class="helpful">
               4 out of 5 people found this review helpful.

             <td>
              <div class="postdate">
              </div>
              <h3>
               <span class="itmRating">
                <img alt="5 out of 5 eggs" class="eggs r5" src="http://images10.newegg.com/WebResource/Themes/2005/Nest/none.gif"/>
                <span class="print" style="display:none;">
                 Rating: 5/5
                </span>
               </span>
               Beauty
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                I got this monitor on sale for $550. It was a big price to pay, and I had a lot of hesitation going in. I'm a college student on a budget, but I wanted a nice monitor. Studying to work on Game Design, I wanted something to perform the following:
                <br/>
                - Have accurate color reproduction
                <br/>
                - Have multiple inputs (Not going into this further for obv. reasons)
                <br/>
                - Have little to no ghosting
                <br/>
                - Have LOTS of screen real estate.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                I was going to get the 29" right as this beauty went on sale. Here it is, about 2 months later, and I do not regret splurging on this whatsoever.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                For gaming, there is little to no ghosting. I play Guild Wars 2, and this monitor is an outstanding addition. It's totally immersive as it fills nearly your entire field of vision (or, at least, what you generally pay attention to. It won't fill all of your peripheral).
                <br/>
                <br/>
                I then fired up Photoshop and Unity, configuring setups. I found nice setups with both... with room to spare! The 21:9 ratio, I feel, helped a lot.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                The color, also, was BEAUTIFUL when the brightness was high enough. I tend to turn it down to minimum brightness when I'm just staring at a wall of text or doing school work, but when working with color or playing a game, setting the brightness to ~30-40 percent gives an amazing experience.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                ...Even now I'm still impressed that an IPS panel has so little ghosting.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                In regards to the cons... I'd like to start by saying this line.
                <br/>
                21:9 is NOT for everyone.
                <br/>
                21 by 9 is NOT for everyone.
                <br/>
                21:9 IS NOT FOR EVERYONE.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                For me, it was a perfect fit. However, I'd recommend weighing your options first. Due to the nature of screen measurements, this monitor doesn't have as much vertical height as you might expect initially. Find some online calculators and find the actual width and height of the monitors you're considering. This monitor has the height of... I believe it was a 27" 16:9 monitor. Don't quote me on that, though. I didn't actually do the math for it at the time of writing to double check the validity of that statement.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Another thing to consider is the overall size. Consider your desk. Will this beast fit? It's thin, but it's still huge. The panel itself is 31.25 inches WIDE. Then add the bezel. (The height is about 13 and a half inches or so, by the way).
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                I almost regret not getting the 34UM95 instead, but I don't think my little GTX 660 could power that in games well enough for it to be enjoyable. If you have the graphics horsepower, save up for an extra few weeks and get the um95 instead, because you can see the pixels on this monitor if you get close enough.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Also, if you fall in love with 21:9, you'll never want to return to 16:9 or 16:10, and 4:3 will look absolutely abysmal. I don't think I can ever personally return to using 16:9 as my daily driver. The extra width is the best thing I could have asked for.
               </p>
              </div>
              <p class="helpful">
               2 out of 2 people found this review helpful.

              <h3>
               <span class="itmRating">
                <img alt="5 out of 5 eggs" class="eggs r5" src="http://images10.newegg.com/WebResource/Themes/2005/Nest/none.gif"/>
                <span class="print" style="display:none;">
                 Rating: 5/5
                </span>
               </span>
               Don't Buy 3 Monitors, Buy This One
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                When I first saw the Curved version of this Monitor I quickly fell in love with the 21:9 Screens. Based on what I could afford I went with the 34UM65-P. Not One Regret. I had a TV and 2 Monitors prior, this Monitor Rocks. I am able to split the screen into 3 screens as if I had 3 Monitors. It is a beautiful display, I love being able to watch newer movies at 21:9, it fills the whole screen, No Bars. This Monitor even has its own speakers which are ok if you don't have any speakers. Now onto Gaming, I have a 760 video card and everything from BF4, Crysis 3 to Titanfall works Perfectly filling the whole screen, very smooth, no noticeable lagging. I went from a 2ms Monitor to this 5ms and truthfully I cannot see a difference. Maybe it is the Awe of this big screen. All games mentioned I am able to set them to the Highest settings at 2560 x 1080. Doing the Math, I was looking at getting another 3 monitor type setup but I am so glad I had this option for around the same cost of the 3 monitors. Again, No Regrets. If you can afford the 34UM95-P or the Curved 34UC97-S Great, but in my opinion, this is the best monitor for the price. You could get two of these for what the 34UC97-S cost. Oh, I highly recommend only connecting this Monitor to a Gaming card by a Display Port Cable.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                None
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                Just be prepared to have everyone who sees this monitor say, Wow...Oh and yes I have this same review on LG's site.
               </p>
              </div>

              <h3>
               <span class="itmRating">
                <img alt="5 out of 5 eggs" class="eggs r5" src="http://images10.newegg.com/WebResource/Themes/2005/Nest/none.gif"/>
                <span class="print" style="display:none;">
                 Rating: 5/5
                </span>
               </span>
               Amazing Moniter
              </h3>
              <div class="details">
               <div class="review-title" style="display: none">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  This review is from:
                 </strong>
                 LG 34UM65 Black 34" 5ms(GTG) Dual HDMI 21:9 UltraWide LED Backlight LCD Monitor IPS Panel 300 cd/m2 DFC 5,000,000:1(1000:1) Built-in Speakers
                </p>
               </div>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Pros:
                </em>
                I love this monitor, coming from a 42 720p tv this thing is a dream. Its colors are amazing straight out of the box and i have no back light bleed at all. I use this on games like Guild wars 2, WoW, The Crew, and League of legends and it is fantastic. I plan on buying the larger resolution model in the future
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Cons:
                </em>
                The one thing i didn't like is that for some reason i got a Japanese model so i have no English menus....not sure why but i came with a power adapter so its not that pig of a deal and i found a pdf of the manual on Lgs website.
               </p>
               <p>
                <em>
                 Other Thoughts:
                </em>
                Amazing for immersive game play and not much harder to run than a 16:9 1080p moniter. Defiantly worth picking up if you look into immersion or even productivity
               </p>
              </div>
              <p class="helpful">
               1 out of 1 people found this review helpful.

                Did you?

    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
     usingNamespace("Biz.Common")["RecentlyView2012"] = function () {
            var hasBloomReach = 1;
            var moduleType = 2;
            var getParameters = function () {
                var viewItems = Web.StateManager.Cookies.get(Web.StateManager.Cookies.Name.PRDLIST, "ItemViewed");
                if (viewItems) {
                    if (Web.Config.RecentlyViewPrimaryItem) {
                        return "v=" + viewItems.split("#").join(",") + "&amp;item=" + Web.Config.RecentlyViewPrimaryItem;
                    }
                    return "v=" + viewItems.split("#").join(",");
                };
                return "";
            };
            return {
                getData: function () {
                    var script = $("recentlyView2012AjaxJS");
                    if (script &amp;&amp; script != null) {
                        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].removeChild(script);
                    }
                    script = document.createElement("script");
                    script.type = "text/javascript";
                    script.id = 'recentlyView2012AjaxJS';
                    script.src = Web.UI.ResourceManager.Url.www("Common/Ajax/RecentlyView2012.aspx") + "?" + getParameters() + "&amp;type=" + moduleType;
                    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
                },
                renderData: function (pData) {
                    if (pData.length &gt; 0) {
                        if (moduleType == 0) {
                            document.getElementById("boxViewed").innerHTML = pData;
                        } else {
                            var content = jQuery(pData);
                            var recentlyViewed = content.length&gt;0? jQuery(content[0]):null;
                            var recentlySearch = content.length&gt;1? jQuery(content[1]):null;
                            if (recentlyViewed) {
                                jQuery("#recentlyViewed2013").attr("class", recentlyViewed.attr("class")).html(recentlyViewed.html()).css("display","");
                            }
                            if (recentlySearch) {
                                jQuery("#recentlySearch2013").attr("class", recentlySearch.attr("class")).html(recentlySearch.html()).css("display", "");
                            }
                            if(!recentlyViewed &amp;&amp; !hasBloomReach){
                                jQuery("#boxViewedContent").css("display","none");
                            }
                        }
                    };
                    var loader = document.getElementById("loader_recentlyView");
                    if (loader) {
                        loader.style.display = "none";
                    }
                }
            };
        }();
        Biz.Common.RecentlyView2012.getData();
    </script>
